{

    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;

    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat6);

    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat11 + 0.125;

    u_xlat0 = u_xlat16_35 / u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 * u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 * u_xlat4.x;
    u_xlat0 = min(u_xlat0, 100.0);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = clamp(u_xlat0, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat7.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = min(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat10_4.w * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat10_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat10_3.w + _AlphaOffset;
    u_xlat16_32 = clamp(u_xlat16_32, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_0.w = u_xlat16_32 * _CustomAlpha;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _EmisssionColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat10_4.zzz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat4.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;
    u_xlat4.y = _TimeParameters.x * _OverlayColorQuency;
    u_xlat4.xy = sin(u_xlat4.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = _OverlayColor.w + (-_OverlayColorFlicker);
    u_xlat16_35 = _OverlayColor.w + _OverlayColorFlicker;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 + (-u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat4.y * u_xlat16_32 + u_xlat16_35;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_32) * _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = _OverlayColor.xyz * vec3(_Ratio_OverlayColorEffect) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_32 = log2(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_32 * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_32 = exp2(u_xlat16_32);
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_35 = exp2(u_xlat16_35);
    u_xlat16_35 = min(u_xlat16_35, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.x = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat4.x * u_xlat16_8.x + _DOTEmissionMax;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_8.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _flowFresnelColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _flowColor.xyz * _flowColor.www + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_35 * _DOTEmissionScale;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_32 * _Ratio_FlashColorEffect;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat24 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat4.xy = vec2(u_xlat24) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat10_4.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat4.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.300000012, 0.300000012, 0.300000012) + vec3(0.699999988, 0.699999988, 0.699999988);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.w = (-u_xlat16_1.x) * 1.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.w = clamp(u_xlat16_3.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = (-u_xlat16_0) + u_xlat16_3;
    u_xlat16_0 = vec4(vec4(_WhiteFresnelAlpha, _WhiteFresnelAlpha, _WhiteFresnelAlpha, _WhiteFresnelAlpha)) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz / u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = min(u_xlat4.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    return;

    u_xlat15.x = _Time.x * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.y;

    u_xlat0.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = cos(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = sin(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat3.yz = u_xlat0.xx;

    u_xlat15.y = dot(u_xlat12.yx, u_xlat3.xy);

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;

in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat7;
vec2 u_xlat12;
float u_xlat13;
vec2 u_xlat15;
float u_xlat18;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainAnimationMap_ST.xy + _MainAnimationMap_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat7;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat7);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat13 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat4.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD11.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD11.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat3.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD11.y = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat16_2.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.z + _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.x * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = cos(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat3.y = sin((-u_xlat0.x));
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(2.0, 2.0) + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat12.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.z * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = sin(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat4.x = cos(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat4.yz = u_xlat3.xx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * vec3(0.5, -0.5, 0.5) + vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat12.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat12.xy, u_xlat3.xz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat12.yx, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat4.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * _MixMapUVDataLayerR.xy + _MixMapUVDataLayerR.zw;
    u_xlat15.x = _Time.x * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xy = u_xlat15.xx * u_xlat0.xy + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = cos(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = sin(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat3.yz = u_xlat0.xx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(0.5, -0.5, 0.5) + vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat15.x = dot(u_xlat12.xy, u_xlat3.xz);
    u_xlat15.y = dot(u_xlat12.yx, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat15.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * _MixMapUVDataLayerG.xy + _MixMapUVDataLayerG.zw;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z + _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.x;
    u_xlat12.x = u_xlat16_2.x * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat15.x = cos(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat15.y = sin((-u_xlat12.x));
    u_xlat12.xy = u_xlat15.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat12.xy = u_xlat12.xy * vec2(2.0, 2.0) + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.x = _Time.x * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.zw = u_xlat3.xx * u_xlat12.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD11.w = 0.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _AdditionalTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMap;

UNITY_LOCATION(6) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixAnimationMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
float u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump float u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
float u_xlat14;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
float u_xlat24;
vec2 u_xlat26;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
mediump float u_xlat16_32;
mediump float u_xlat16_33;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = max(u_xlat0, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0 = inversesqrt(u_xlat0);
    u_xlat10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot((-u_xlat10.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_31)) + (-u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = abs(u_xlat16_31) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_32 = max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_33 = (-u_xlat16_32) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_3 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35 + 1.0;
    u_xlat10.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat10.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_5.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3

    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat13 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat4.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD11.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD11.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat3.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD11.y = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat16_2.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.z + _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.x * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = cos(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat3.y = sin((-u_xlat0.x));
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(2.0, 2.0) + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat12.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.z * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = sin(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat4.x = cos(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat4.yz = u_xlat3.xx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * vec3(0.5, -0.5, 0.5) + vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat12.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat12.xy, u_xlat3.xz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat12.yx, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat4.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * _MixMapUVDataLayerR.xy + _MixMapUVDataLayerR.zw;
    u_xlat15.x = _Time.x * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xy = u_xlat15.xx * u_xlat0.xy + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = cos(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = sin(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat3.yz = u_xlat0.xx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(0.5, -0.5, 0.5) + vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat15.x = dot(u_xlat12.xy, u_xlat3.xz);
    u_xlat15.y = dot(u_xlat12.yx, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat15.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * _MixMapUVDataLayerG.xy + _MixMapUVDataLayerG.zw;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z + _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.x;
    u_xlat12.x = u_xlat16_2.x * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat15.x = cos(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat15.y = sin((-u_xlat12.x));
    u_xlat12.xy = u_xlat15.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat12.xy = u_xlat12.xy * vec2(2.0, 2.0) + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.x = _Time.x * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.zw = u_xlat3.xx * u_xlat12.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD11.w = 0.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat17.x = min(max(u_xlat17.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat16_38 = min(max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0), 1.0);

    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;

    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_39 * _DOTFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_39 = exp2(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_39 = min(u_xlat16_39, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = exp2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(u_xlat16_6.x, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_18.x = (-_DOTEmissionMax) + _DOTEmissionMin;

    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_32) * _DOTColor.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xy = vs_TEXCOORD8.xy * _AddTexST.xy + _AddTexST.zw;
    u_xlat24 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat4.xy = vec2(u_xlat24) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat10_4.xyz = texture2D(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat4.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat10_4.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_32 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_9.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.300000012, 0.300000012, 0.300000012) + vec3(0.699999988, 0.699999988, 0.699999988);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_3.w = (-u_xlat16_1.x) * 1.5 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.w = clamp(u_xlat16_3.w, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_1 = (-u_xlat16_0) + u_xlat16_3;
    u_xlat16_0 = vec4(vec4(_WhiteFresnelAlpha, _WhiteFresnelAlpha, _WhiteFresnelAlpha, _WhiteFresnelAlpha)) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);

    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz / u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = min(u_xlat4.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));

void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;

    u_xlat0 = max(u_xlat0, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0 = inversesqrt(u_xlat0);
    u_xlat10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot((-u_xlat10.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_31)) + (-u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = abs(u_xlat16_31) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MixMapColorLayerR;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MixMapColorLayerG;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AlphaOffset;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
float u_xlat7;
vec2 u_xlat12;
float u_xlat13;
vec2 u_xlat15;
float u_xlat18;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainAnimationMap_ST.xy + _MainAnimationMap_ST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat0.y * u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat7 = u_xlat0.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + u_xlat7;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * 0.125 + (-u_xlat7);
    u_xlat1.y = u_xlat1.x + 0.125;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat13 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_2.xy = max(u_xlat1.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_1 = u_xlat16_2.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = (-u_xlat4.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat5.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat3.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD11.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD11.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat3.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD11.y = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat3.x = min(max(u_xlat3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat3.x = clamp(u_xlat3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.z + _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.x * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = cos(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat3.y = sin((-u_xlat0.x));
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(2.0, 2.0) + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat12.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.z * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = sin(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat4.x = cos(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat4.yz = u_xlat3.xx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * vec3(0.5, -0.5, 0.5) + vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat12.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat12.xy, u_xlat3.xz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat12.yx, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat4.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * _MixMapUVDataLayerR.xy + _MixMapUVDataLayerR.zw;
    u_xlat15.x = _Time.x * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xy = u_xlat15.xx * u_xlat0.xy + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = cos(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = sin(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat3.yz = u_xlat0.xx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(0.5, -0.5, 0.5) + vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat15.x = dot(u_xlat12.xy, u_xlat3.xz);
    u_xlat15.y = dot(u_xlat12.yx, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat15.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * _MixMapUVDataLayerG.xy + _MixMapUVDataLayerG.zw;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z + _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.x;
    u_xlat12.x = u_xlat16_2.x * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat15.x = cos(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat15.y = sin((-u_xlat12.x));
    u_xlat12.xy = u_xlat15.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat12.xy = u_xlat12.xy * vec2(2.0, 2.0) + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.x = _Time.x * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.zw = u_xlat3.xx * u_xlat12.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD11.w = 0.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD8;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
float u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
mediump float u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
vec3 u_xlat10;
float u_xlat14;
mediump float u_xlat16_14;
mediump float u_xlat16_15;
float u_xlat24;
vec2 u_xlat26;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
mediump float u_xlat16_32;
mediump float u_xlat16_33;
mediump float u_xlat16_35;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_BumpMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = u_xlat16_1.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xyw;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_2.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_2.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat0 = max(u_xlat0, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0 = inversesqrt(u_xlat0);
    u_xlat10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat0) * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot((-u_xlat10.xyz), u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_31)) + (-u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, u_xlat10.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = abs(u_xlat16_31) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_4.y + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_32 = max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_33 = (-u_xlat16_32) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_3 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat10.x = u_xlat16_35 * u_xlat16_35 + 1.0;
    u_xlat10.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat10.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat10.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x + _MetallicOffset;
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_5.x) * 0.959999979 + 0.959999979;
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_5.x = min(max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_5.x = clamp(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_15) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15 = (-u_xlat16_32) + u_xlat16_15;
    u_xlat4.x = u_xlat16_32 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_15 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_32 = min(max(u_xlat16_32, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_32 = clamp(u_xlat16_32, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6.xy = vs_TEXCOORD11.xy / vs_TEXCOORD11.zz;
    u_xlat26.xy = (-u_xlat6.xy) * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.ww + vs_TEXCOORD9.xy;
    u_xlat6.xy = (-u_xlat6.xy) * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.ww + vs_TEXCOORD9.zw;
    u_xlat16_14 = texture(_MixAnimationMap, u_xlat6.xy).y;
    u_xlat16_6 = texture(_MixAnimationMap, u_xlat26.xy).x;
    u_xlat16_7.x = u_xlat16_6 + -0.5;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_6) * _MixMapColorLayerR.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.y = (-u_xlat16_14) + 0.5;
    u_xlat6.xy = u_xlat16_7.xy * vec2(vec2(_MixMapDistortionScale, _MixMapDistortionScale)) + vs_TEXCOORD0.zw;
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_MainAnimationMap, u_xlat6.xy);
    u_xlat16_15 = u_xlat16_3.w + _MainMapAlphaMaskOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_15 = min(max(u_xlat16_15, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_15 = clamp(u_xlat16_15, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_15);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _MainColor.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_14) * _MixMapColorLayerG.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;

    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat1.yzx;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat1.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD11.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD11.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat3.z;
    vs_TEXCOORD11.y = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat4.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat4.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat4.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat0.z * unity_FogParams.z + unity_FogParams.w;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat3.x = min(max(u_xlat3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat3.x = clamp(u_xlat3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    gl_Position = u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.x = u_xlat3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.yzw = vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.z + _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_2.x * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = cos(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat3.y = sin((-u_xlat0.x));
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat3.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * vec2(2.0, 2.0) + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat12.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.z * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = sin(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat4.x = cos(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat4.yz = u_xlat3.xx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * vec3(0.5, -0.5, 0.5) + vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat12.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy + vec2(-0.5, -0.5);
    u_xlat4.x = dot(u_xlat12.xy, u_xlat3.xz);
    u_xlat4.y = dot(u_xlat12.yx, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat4.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xy = u_xlat3.xy * _MixMapUVDataLayerR.xy + _MixMapUVDataLayerR.zw;
    u_xlat15.x = _Time.x * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xy = u_xlat15.xx * u_xlat0.xy + u_xlat3.xy;
    u_xlat0.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat3.x = cos(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.x = sin(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat3.yz = u_xlat0.xx;
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(0.5, -0.5, 0.5) + vec3(0.5, 0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat15.x = dot(u_xlat12.xy, u_xlat3.xz);
    u_xlat15.y = dot(u_xlat12.yx, u_xlat3.xy);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat15.xy + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat0.xy = u_xlat0.xy * _MixMapUVDataLayerG.xy + _MixMapUVDataLayerG.zw;
    u_xlat16_2.x = _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.z + _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.x;
    u_xlat12.x = u_xlat16_2.x * 6.28318548;
    u_xlat15.x = cos(u_xlat12.x);
    u_xlat15.y = sin((-u_xlat12.x));
    u_xlat12.xy = u_xlat15.xy * vec2(0.5, 0.5) + vec2(0.5, 0.5);
    u_xlat12.xy = u_xlat12.xy * vec2(2.0, 2.0) + vec2(-1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat3.x = _Time.x * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.zw = u_xlat3.xx * u_xlat12.xy + u_xlat0.xy;
    vs_TEXCOORD11.w = 0.0;
    return;
}

{
    u_xlat0.xy = vs_TEXCOORD11.xy / vs_TEXCOORD11.zz;
    u_xlat24.xy = (-u_xlat0.xy) * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerR.ww + vs_TEXCOORD9.xy;
    u_xlat0.xy = (-u_xlat0.xy) * _MixMapAnimationDataLayerG.ww + vs_TEXCOORD9.zw;

    u_xlat16_12 = texture(_MixAnimationMap, u_xlat24.xy).x;

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_12) * _MixMapColorLayerR.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.y = (-u_xlat16_0.x) + 0.5;

#else

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_38 = min(max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

#endif

    u_xlat16_38 = _MetallicOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_38 = min(max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

#endif

    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat4.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_2.xy = u_xlat16_2.xy * vec2(vec2(_NormalScale, _NormalScale));

    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_2.xyw;

    u_xlat16_38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_38);

    u_xlat40 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat40 = min(max(u_xlat40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat40 = clamp(u_xlat40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat40);
    u_xlat16_7.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_7.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_7.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;

    u_xlat5.x = max(u_xlat5.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat5.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat5.x);

    u_xlat8.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat8.x);
    u_xlat17.xyz = u_xlat17.xyz * u_xlat8.xxx;
    u_xlat17.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat17.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat17.x = min(max(u_xlat17.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat17.x = clamp(u_xlat17.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat29 = (-u_xlat17.x) * u_xlat17.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = _RoughNessOffset + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0399999991);

    u_xlat17.x = u_xlat17.x * u_xlat29;
    u_xlat17.x = min(u_xlat17.x, 100.0);

    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);

    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_11.xyz;

    u_xlat16_38 = (-u_xlat16_38) + u_xlat16_39;

#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_38 = min(max(u_xlat16_38, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

    u_xlat40 = (-u_xlat16_38) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat40 * u_xlat40;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_39) * u_xlat17.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat4.x = _TimeParameters.x * _DOTEmissionQuency;

    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_39 * _flowFresnelPower;
    u_xlat16_39 = exp2(u_xlat16_39);
    u_xlat16_39 = min(u_xlat16_39, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.x = exp2(u_xlat16_6.x);
    u_xlat16_6.x = min(u_xlat16_6.x, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_6.x * _DOTEmissionScale;

    u_xlat28 = fract(_Time.x);
    u_xlat4.xy = vec2(u_xlat28) * _flowPosition.zw + u_xlat4.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = texture(_AdditionalTexture, u_xlat4.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * _AddTexColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = _Ratio_ExtraTexture * _AddTexScale;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_10.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_39) + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_18.xyz * vec3(vec3(_Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor, _Ratio_flowColor)) + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * _SteadyColor.xyz + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = _Ratio_SteadyColorEffect * _SteadyColor.w;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.300000012, 0.300000012, 0.300000012) + vec3(0.699999988, 0.699999988, 0.699999988);
    u_xlat16_38 = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat16_7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_38 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_38);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_38) * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.w = (-u_xlat16_2.x) * 1.5 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.w = min(max(u_xlat16_1.w, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.w = clamp(u_xlat16_1.w, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1 = (-u_xlat16_0) + u_xlat16_1;
    u_xlat16_0 = vec4(_WhiteFresnelAlpha) * u_xlat16_1 + u_xlat16_0;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.12949991, 1.12949991, 1.12949991) + vec3(0.0299999993, 0.0299999993, 0.0299999993);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(0.449999988, 0.449999988, 0.449999988);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(1.09350002, 1.09350002, 1.09350002) + vec3(0.589999974, 0.589999974, 0.589999974);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_0.w;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat5.xyz + vec3(0.0799999982, 0.0799999982, 0.0799999982);
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz / u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = min(u_xlat4.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    SV_Target0.xyz = u_xlat4.xyz;
    return;
}

#endif
"

 Pass {
  Name "UBuffEffect"
  LOD 300
  Tags { "IGNOREPROJECTOR" = "true" "LIGHTMODE" = "UBuffEffect" "QUEUE" = "Geometry+550" "RenderPipeline" = "LightweightPipeline" "RenderType" = "Transparent" }

Program "vp" {
SubProgram "gles " {
"// hash: 2ae351e8acbca6e3
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
varying highp float vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xyz = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

{
    u_xlat0.x = _Time.y * _LineColorSpeed + _LineColorPosi;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.y = 0.5;
    u_xlat10_0.xyz = texture2D(_LineColor, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz + (-_LineConstColor.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(_TexorColor) * u_xlat0.xyz + _LineConstColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = (-vs_TEXCOORD0) + 1.0;
    u_xlat1 = log2(u_xlat1);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 * _Rim;
    u_xlat1 = exp2(u_xlat1);
    u_xlat1 = min(u_xlat1, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1 * _CustomAlpha;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

#define HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS 1
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
#define UNITY_UNIFORM
#else
#define UNITY_UNIFORM uniform
#endif
#define UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION 1
#if UNITY_SUPPORTS_UNIFORM_LOCATION
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x) layout(location = x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(binding = x, std140)
#else
#define UNITY_LOCATION(x)
#define UNITY_BINDING(x) layout(std140)
#endif
uniform 	vec4 _Time;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(0) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _LineColorPosi;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _LineColorSpeed;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec3 _LineConstColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _TexorColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _CustomAlpha;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _Offset1;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _Offset2;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _UBuffWidth;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _OutlineColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _lightDir;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Rim;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump sampler2D _LineColor;
in highp float vs_TEXCOORD0;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_0;
float u_xlat1;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = _Time.y * _LineColorSpeed + _LineColorPosi;
    u_xlat0.x = fract(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.y = 0.5;
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = texture(_LineColor, u_xlat0.xy).xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz + (-_LineConstColor.xyz);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(_TexorColor) * u_xlat0.xyz + _LineConstColor.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = (-vs_TEXCOORD0) + 1.0;
    u_xlat1 = log2(u_xlat1);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 * _Rim;
    u_xlat1 = exp2(u_xlat1);
    u_xlat1 = min(u_xlat1, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.w = u_xlat1 * _CustomAlpha;
    SV_Target0 = u_xlat0;
    return;
}

#endif
"
}

"// hash: 646e16e91365991e
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec3 _WorldSpaceCameraPos;
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	float _Offset1;
uniform 	float _Offset2;
uniform 	float _UBuffWidth;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec4 in_COLOR0;
varying highp float vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = ceil(in_COLOR0.w);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + in_COLOR0.w;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat0.x = (-u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.0500000007;
    u_xlat2.x = _Offset1 + _Offset2;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat2.x * 0.00999999978 + (-u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat2.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, in_NORMAL0.xyz);
    u_xlat2.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xxx * in_NORMAL0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(vec3(_UBuffWidth, _UBuffWidth, _UBuffWidth)) + in_POSITION0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat2.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * u_xlat2.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * u_xlat2.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat2.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat2.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat2.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat2.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x / u_xlat1.w;
    gl_Position.z = (-u_xlat0.x) + u_xlat1.z;
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat1.xyw;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat0.xyz);
    return;
}

#endif

 Pass {
  Name "ShadowCaster"
  LOD 300
  Tags { "IGNOREPROJECTOR" = "true" "LIGHTMODE" = "SHADOWCASTER" "QUEUE" = "Geometry+550" "RenderPipeline" = "LightweightPipeline" "RenderType" = "Transparent" }
  GpuProgramID 230925
Program "vp" {
SubProgram "gles " {
"// hash: 7e1f6e5f7ab0171f
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowBias;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
uniform 	vec3 _LightDirection;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionMin;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _OverlayColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OverlayColorQuency;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _OverlayColorFlicker;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_OverlayColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _DOTEmissionScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_OverlayColorEffect;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MouthTiling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MouthOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EyeTiling;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EyeOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _AddTexST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _AddTexColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _AddTexScale;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_ExtraTexture;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowPosition;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _flowFresnelPower;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _flowFresnelColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _flowFilp;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Ratio_flowColor;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _PostUVFlip;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _FaceOffset;
	UNITY_UNIFORM float _ChangeFace;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _EmisssionColor;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

#endif
#ifdef FRAGMENT
#version 300 es

precision highp float;
precision highp int;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_TARGET0;
void main()
{
    SV_TARGET0 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    return;
}

#endif
"
}
}
